         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            Say I'm in a Git repository. I delete a file and commit that change. I continue working and make some more commits. Then, I find I need to restore that file.
           </p>
           <p>
            I know I can checkout a file using
            <code>
             git checkout HEAD^ foo.bar
            </code>
            , but I don't really know when that file was deleted.
           </p>
           <ol>
            <li>
             What would be the quickest way to find the commit that deleted a given filename?
            </li>
            <li>
             What would be the easiest way to get that file back into my working copy?
            </li>
           </ol>
           <p>
            I'm hoping I don't have to manually browse my logs, checkout the entire project for a given SHA and then manually copy that file into my original project checkout.
           </p>
          </div>

               <span class="comment-copy">
                @hhh
                <code>
                 git checkout deletedFile
                </code>
                will undelete
                <code>
                 deletedFile
                </code>
                if it's been deleted but that deletion
                <i>
                 has not yet been staged or committed
                </i>
                . That's not what the question here is asking for; this question is about how to restore a file whose deletion was committed many commits ago.
               </span>
               <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

        <a name="1113140">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="1113140" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3390" id="answer-1113140" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="1113140">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3390" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3390
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/1113140/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Find the last commit that affected the given path. As the file isn't in the HEAD commit, that previous commit must have deleted it.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- &lt;file_path&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Then checkout the version at the commit before, using the caret (
             <code>
              ^
             </code>
             ) symbol:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout &lt;deleting_commit&gt;^ -- &lt;file_path&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Or in one command, if
             <code>
              $file
             </code>
             is the file in question.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- "$file")^ -- "$file"
</code></pre>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             If you are using zsh and have the EXTENDED_GLOB option enabled, the caret symbol won't work. You can use
             <code>
              ~1
             </code>
             instead.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- "$file")~1 -- "$file"
</code></pre>
           </div>

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @zoras zsh has it's own expansion on '^' I believe, but you can use the alternative syntax of '~1':
                 <code>
                  git checkout &lt;deleting-commit&gt;~1 -- &lt;file-path&gt;
                 </code>
                 ~X allows you to specify X commits before the specified commit, so ~1 is the commit before, ~2 is two commits before, etc
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/501130/nils-luxton" title="765 reputation">

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="53156371" data-comment-owner-id="10608" data-comment-score="31" id="comment-53156371">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="supernova" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 31
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 On windows cmd prompt, the
                 <code>
                  ^
                 </code>
                 character is the escape character! Therefore, on cmd, you have to type
                 <code>
                  ^^
                 </code>
                 to tell cmd you want a single literal ^ and that your not escaping something else after it. What's happening to many people is that the
                 <code>
                  ^
                 </code>
                 is followed by a space. So cmd thinks you're escaping the space -- which yields simply a space character. Thus, by the time git gets the cli arguments, it sees
                 <code>
                  SHA1
                 </code>
                 and
                 <b>
                  not
                 </b>
                 <code>
                  SHA1^
                 </code>
                 . It's really annoying.
                 <code>
                  ~
                 </code>
                 isn't an escape character, so that's why that still works. (PS. if you think googlers will want this info, please upvote this comment)
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/10608/alexander-bird" title="36,045 reputation">
                  Alexander Bird
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2015-09-18 14:48:29Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Sep 18, 2015 at 14:48
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="953573">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/953573/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <ol>
             <li>
              Use
              <code>
               git log --diff-filter=D --summary
              </code>
              to get all the commits which have deleted files and the files deleted;
             </li>
             <li>
              Use
              <code>
               git checkout $commit~1 path/to/file.ext
              </code>
              to restore the deleted file.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Where
             <code>
              $commit
             </code>
             is the value of the commit you've found at step 1, e.g.
             <code>
              e4cf499627
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             To restore all those deleted files in a folder, enter the following command.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git ls-files -d | xargs git checkout --
</code></pre>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="22976202">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             142
            </div>

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/22976202/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I came to this question looking to restore a file I just deleted but I hadn't yet committed the change.  Just in case you find yourself in this situation, all you need to do is the following:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git checkout HEAD -- path/to/file.ext
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="953507">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="953507" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="5" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="100" id="answer-953507" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="953507">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="100" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             100
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/953507/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you’re insane, use
             <a href="http://www.kernel.org/pub/software/scm/git/docs/git-bisect.html" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git-bisect
              </code>
             </a>
             . Here's what to do:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git bisect start
git bisect bad
git bisect good &lt;some commit where you know the file existed&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now it's time to run the automated test. The shell command
             <code>
              '[ -e foo.bar ]'
             </code>
             will return 0 if
             <code>
              foo.bar
             </code>
             exists, and 1 otherwise. The "run" command of
             <code>
              git-bisect
             </code>
             will use binary search to automatically find the first commit where the test fails. It starts halfway through the range given (from good to bad) and cuts it in half based on the result of the specified test.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git bisect run '[ -e foo.bar ]'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now you're at the commit which deleted it. From here, you can jump back to the future and use
             <a href="http://www.kernel.org/pub/software/scm/git/docs/git-revert.html" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git-revert
              </code>
             </a>
             to undo the change,
            </p>
            <pre><code>git bisect reset
git revert &lt;the offending commit&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             or you could go back one commit and manually inspect the damage:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout HEAD^
cp foo.bar /tmp
git bisect reset
cp /tmp/foo.bar .
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @avdgaag the
                 <code>
                  git bisect run
                 </code>
                 tells Git to automate bisection by running the command following word 'run' where the command must return
                 <code>
                  0
                 </code>
                 for a
                 <code>
                  good
                 </code>
                 version (see
                 <code>
                  git help bisect
                 </code>
                 for details). The
                 <code>
                  '[ -e foo.bar ]'
                 </code>
                 is a standard expression for testing if file
                 <code>
                  foo.bar
                 </code>
                 does exists (the implementation is usually in file
                 <code>
                  /usr/bin/[
                 </code>
                 which is usually hardlinked to
                 <code>
                  /usr/bin/test
                 </code>
                 ) and the single quation marks are used to put that all as a single command line argument.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/334451/mikko-rantalainen" title="11,353 reputation">
                  Mikko Rantalainen

        <a name="14922749">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="14922749" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="81" id="answer-14922749" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="14922749">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="81" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             81
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/14922749/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             My new favorite alias, based on
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/525305/bonyiii">
              bonyiii
             </a>
             's
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/11301004/6309">
              answer
             </a>
             (upvoted), and my own answer about "
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/7005698/6309">
              Pass an argument to a Git alias command
             </a>
             ":
            </p>
            <pre><code>git config alias.restore '!f() { git checkout $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- $1)~1 -- $(git diff --name-status $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- $1)~1 | grep '^D' | cut -f 2); }; f'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I have lost a file, deleted by mistake a few commits ago?
             <br/>
             Quick:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git restore my_deleted_file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Crisis averted.
            </p>
            <p>
             Warning, with Git 2.23 (Q3 2019) comes the
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/57066072/6309">
              experimental command
             </a>
             named
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/docs/git-restore" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git restore
              </code>
             </a>
             (!).
             <br/>
             So rename this alias (as shown below).
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/157971/robert-dailey">
              Robert Dailey
             </a>
             proposes
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/953481/restore-a-deleted-file-in-a-git-repo/14922749#comment33996752_14922749">
              in the comments
             </a>
             the following alias:
            </p>
            <pre><code>restore-file = !git checkout $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- "$1")^ -- "$1"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/1857677/jegan">
              jegan
             </a>
             adds
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/953481/find-and-restore-a-deleted-file-in-a-git-repository/14922749?noredirect=1#comment80261163_14922749">
              in the comments
             </a>
             :
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              For setting the alias from the command line, I used this command:
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <pre><code>git config --global alias.restore "\!git checkout \$(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- \"\$1\")^ -- \"\$1\"" 
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2013-02-17T15:33:29" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="14922749">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

                 Here is my alias, works wonderfully:
                 <code>
                  restore-file = !git checkout $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- "$1")^ -- "$1"
                 </code>
                </span>

                 For setting the alias from the command line, I used this command:
                 <code>
                  git config --global alias.restore "\!git checkout \$(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- \"\$1\")^ -- \"\$1\""
                 </code>
                </span>

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="35664754" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="65" id="answer-35664754" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35664754">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="65" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             65
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35664754/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you know the filename, this is an easy way with basic commands:
            </p>
            <p>
             List all the commits for that file.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git log -- path/to/file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The last commit (topmost) is the one that deleted the file. So you need to restore the second to last commit.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout {second to last commit} -- path/to/file
</code></pre>
           </div>

                 <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/penultimate#Synonyms" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  en.wiktionary.org/wiki/penultimate#Synonyms
                 </a>
                </span>

        <a name="11322499">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="11322499" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="30" id="answer-11322499" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="11322499">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="30" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             30
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/11322499/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             To restore a deleted and commited file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reset HEAD some/path
git checkout -- some/path
</code></pre>
            <p>
             It was tested on Git version 1.7.5.4.
            </p>
           </div>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 -1; this is wrong. These commands will undo a deletion that
                 <i>
                  hasn't yet been committed
                 </i>
                 (the first one unstages the deletion, if it's staged, and the second one discards unstaged changes to the file), but you're claiming here that they'll restore a
                 <i>
                  committed
                 </i>
                 deletion of the file, which simply isn't true and will fail with an error like that in @wisbucky's comment above.
                </span>

        <a name="9514801">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="9514801" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="27" id="answer-9514801" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="9514801">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="27" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             27
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/9514801/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I've got
             <a href="http://blog.loxal.net/2012/03/git-checkout-get-back-deleted-file-w.html" rel="noreferrer">
              this solution
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Get the id of the commit where the file was deleted using one of the ways below.
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                <code>
                 git log --grep=*word*
                </code>
               </li>
               <li>
                <code>
                 git log -Sword
                </code>
               </li>
               <li>
                <code>
                 git log | grep --context=5 *word*
                </code>
               </li>
               <li>
                <code>
                 git log --stat | grep --context=5 *word*
                </code>
                # recommended if you hardly
remember anything
               </li>
              </ul>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               You should get something like:
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              commit bfe68bd117e1091c96d2976c99b3bcc8310bebe7 Author: Alexander
  Orlov  Date:   Thu May 12 23:44:27 2011
  +0200
             </p>
             <pre><code>replaced deprecated GWT class
- gwtI18nKeySync.sh, an outdated (?, replaced by a Maven goal) I18n generation script
</code></pre>
             <p>
              commit 3ea4e3af253ac6fd1691ff6bb89c964f54802302 Author: Alexander
  Orlov  Date:   Thu May 12 22:10:22 2011
  +0200
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             <em>
              3
             </em>
             . Now using the commit id bfe68bd117e1091c96d2976c99b3bcc8310bebe7 do:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout bfe68bd117e1091c96d2976c99b3bcc8310bebe7^1 yourDeletedFile.java
</code></pre>
            <p>
             As the commit id references the commit where the file was already deleted you need to reference the commit just before bfe68b which you can do by appending
             <code>
              ^1
             </code>
             . This means: give me the commit just before bfe68b.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="39296006">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you only made changes and deleted a file, but not commit it, and now you broke up with your changes
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout -- .
</code></pre>
            <p>
             but your deleted files did not return, you simply do the following command:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout &lt;file_path&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And presto, your file is back.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="53457548" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="11" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="16" id="answer-53457548" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="53457548">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="16" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             16
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/53457548/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Actually, this question is directly about Git, but somebody like me works with GUI tools like the
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JetBrains#WebStorm" rel="noreferrer">
              WebStorm
             </a>
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Version_control" rel="noreferrer">
              VCS
             </a>
             other than knowing about Git CLI commands.
            </p>
            <p>
             I right click on the path that contains the deleted file, and then go to Git and then click on
             <em>
              Show History
             </em>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/7302F.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/7302F.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             The VCS tools show all revisions train and I can see all commits and changes of each of them.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/52bs4.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/52bs4.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Then I select the commits that my friend delete the
             <code>
              PostAd.js
             </code>
             file. now see below:
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/IKZv0.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/IKZv0.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             And now, I can see my desire deleted file. I just double-click on the filename and it recovers.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/UJlso.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/UJlso.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             I know my answer is not Git commands, but it is fast, reliable and easy for beginner and professional developers.
             <strong>
              WebStorm
             </strong>
             VCS tools are awesome and perfect for working with Git and it doesn't need any other plugin or tools.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="44425132" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="13" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="15" id="answer-44425132" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="44425132">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="15" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             15
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/44425132/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h1>
             <code>
              git undelete path/to/file.ext
             </code>
            </h1>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Put this in your
               <code>
                .bash_profile
               </code>
               (or other relevant file that loads when you open a command shell):
              </p>
              <pre><code>git config --global alias.undelete '!sh -c "git checkout $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- $1)^ -- $1" -'
</code></pre>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Then use:
              </p>
              <pre><code>git undelete path/to/file.ext
</code></pre>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             This alias first checks to find the last commit where this file existed, and then does a Git checkout of that file path from that last commit where this file existed.
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/43880999/how-to-create-a-git-alias-with-nested-commands-with-parameters">
              Source
             </a>
             .
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

             </time>

        <a name="13012192">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="13012192" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="14" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="11" id="answer-13012192" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="13012192">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="11" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             11
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/13012192/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In many cases, it can be useful to use
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU_Core_Utilities">
              coreutils
             </a>
             (grep, sed, etc.) in conjunction with Git. I already know these tools quite well, but Git less so. If I wanted to do a search for a deleted file, I would do the following:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git log --raw | grep -B 30 $'D\t.*deleted_file.c'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             When I find the revision/commit:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout &lt;rev&gt;^ -- path/to/refound/deleted_file.c
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Just like others have stated before me.
            </p>
            <p>
             The file will now be restored to the state it had before removal. Remember to re-commit it to the working tree if you want to keep it around.
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I had the same question. Without knowing it, I had created a
             <strong>
              <em>
               dangling commit
              </em>
             </strong>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             List dangling commits
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git fsck --lost-found
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Inspect each dangling commit
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git reset --hard &lt;commit id&gt;
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             My files reappeared when I moved to the dangling commit.
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git status
             </code>
             for the reason:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              “HEAD detached from &lt;commit id where it detached&gt;”
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="57809290">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="57809290" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="16" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="7" id="answer-57809290" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="57809290">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="7" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             7
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/57809290/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Find the commit that deleted your file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git log --diff-filter=D --oneline -- path/to/file | cut -f -d ' '
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Sample output:
            </p>
            <pre><code>4711174
</code></pre>
            <p>
             As of Git 2.23 there is actually a
             <code>
              restore
             </code>
             command. It is
             <strong>
              still experimental
             </strong>
             but in order to restore something you removed in a commit (4711174 in this case) you can then type:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git restore --source=4711174^ path/to/file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Note the
             <strong>
              ^
             </strong>
             after the commit id as we want to restore something from the commit
             <strong>
              before
             </strong>
             the one that deleted the file.
            </p>
            <p>
             The
             <code>
              --source
             </code>
             argument tells the
             <code>
              restore
             </code>
             command where to look for the file(s) to restore and it can be any commit and even the index.
            </p>
            <p>
             See:
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/docs/git-restore/2.23.0" rel="noreferrer">
              git-restore doc for git 2.23.0
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="20292699">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/20292699/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I had to restore a bunch of deleted files from a specific commit, and I managed it with two commands:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git show &lt;rev&gt; --diff-filter=D --summary --name-only --no-commit-id | xargs git checkout &lt;rev&gt;^ -- 
git show &lt;rev&gt; --diff-filter=D --summary --name-only --no-commit-id | xargs git reset HEAD 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <em>
              (Note the trailing space on the end of each command.)
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             The files had been added to the .gitignore file and then cleared with
             <code>
              git rm
             </code>
             . I needed to restore the files, but then unstage them. I had hundreds of files to restore, and typing things manually for each file as in the other examples was going to be far too slow.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="13630394">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

              </path>
             </svg>

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/13630394/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>user@bsd:~/work/git$ rm slides.tex
user@bsd:~/work/git$ git pull 
Already up-to-date.
user@bsd:~/work/git$ ls slides.tex
ls: slides.tex: No such file or directory
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Restore the deleted file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>user@bsd:~/work/git$ git checkout
D       .slides.tex.swp
D       slides.tex
user@bsd:~/work/git$ git checkout slides.tex 
user@bsd:~/work/git$ ls slides.tex
slides.tex
</code></pre>
           </div>

          <div class="post-layout--right js-post-comments-component">

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 The question was about restoring a file after it has been deleted and the change has been committed. This answer is about restoring a file which was removed only in the working directory.
                </span>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="11301004" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="19" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="5" id="answer-11301004" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="11301004">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/11301004/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In our case we accidentally deleted files in a commit and some commits later we realized our mistake and wanted to get back all the files that were deleted, but not those that were modified.
            </p>
            <p>
             Based on Charles Bailey's excellent answer, here is my one-liner:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git co $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- &lt;file_path&gt;)~1 -- $(git diff --name-status $(git rev-list -n 1 HEAD -- &lt;file_path&gt;)~1 head | grep '^D' | cut -f 2)
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2012-07-02T20:52:39" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="11301004">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

        <a name="34056090">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="34056090" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="20" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-34056090" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="34056090">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/34056090/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you know the commit that deleted the file(s), run this command where
             <code>
              &lt;SHA1_deletion&gt;
             </code>
             is the commit that deleted the file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git diff --diff-filter=D --name-only &lt;SHA1_deletion&gt;~1 &lt;SHA1_deletion&gt; | xargs git checkout &lt;SHA1_deletion&gt;~1 --
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The part before the pipe lists all the files that were deleted in the  commit; they are all checkout from the previous commit to restore them.
            </p>
           </div>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/53002886/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Simple and precise-
            </p>
            <p>
             First of all, get a latest stable commit in which you have that file by -
            </p>
            <pre><code>git log 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Say you find $commitid 1234567..., then
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout &lt;$commitid&gt; $fileName
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This will restore the file version which was in that commit.
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For the best way to do that, try it.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             First, find the commit id of the commit that deleted your file.
It will give you a summary of commits which deleted files.
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              git log --diff-filter=D --summary
             </p>
             <p>
              git checkout 84sdhfddbdddf~1
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Note:
             <code>
              84sdhfddbddd
             </code>
             is your
             <code>
              commit id
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Through this you can easily recover all deleted files.
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="67763350">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="67763350" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="953481" data-position-on-page="23" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3" id="answer-67763350" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="67763350">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/67763350/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <em>
              <strong>
               Plus point:
              </strong>
              The below methods does work good for the scenario that files/folders got deleted even from your Trash or Recycle bin.
             </em>
            </p>
            <h3>
             Files/Folders are deleted from working tree but not committed yet:
            </h3>
            <p>
             I. If you have not yet indexed (git add) your changes you can revert content of a directory:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git restore -- path/to/folder_OR_file
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             II. If the deletion is already indexed, you should reset that first:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git reset -- path/to/folder_OR_file
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             then perform,
             <code>
              git restore path/to/folder_OR_file
             </code>
            </p>
            <h3>
             Files/Folders are deleted in some commit in the past:
            </h3>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Use
              <code>
               git log --diff-filter=D --summary
              </code>
              to get details of the commits in which files/folder were deleted;
             </li>
             <li>
              Use
              <code>
               git checkout $commit~1 path/to/folder_OR_file
              </code>
              to restore the deleted files/folder.
Where
              <code>
               $commit
              </code>
              is the sha-value of the commit you've found at step 1, e.g. c7578994
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2021-05-30T16:18:37" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="67763350">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">
